## Operational semantics

Simultaneous substitution, a la McBride

  <a id="Value.Fun"></a><a id="4348" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#4348" class="InductiveConstructor">Fun</a> <a id="4352" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4354" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="4356" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4357" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#4357" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="4359" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#4359" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="4361" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#4361" class="Bound">B</a><a id="4362" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4364" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4365" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#4365" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="4367" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4369" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#4357" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="4371" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#1025" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4373" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#4359" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="4375" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#1203" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="4377" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#4361" class="Bound">B</a><a id="4378" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="4386" class="Comment">---------------------------</a>
    <a id="4418" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4420" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#4159" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="4426" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4427" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#1291" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="4429" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#4365" class="Bound">N</a><a id="4430" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Here `zero` requires an implicit parameter to aid inference (much in the same way that `[]` did in [Lists]({{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/Lists.md %})).

  <a id="_⟶_.β-μ"></a><a id="5549" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#5549" class="InductiveConstructor">β-μ</a> <a id="5553" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5555" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="5557" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5558" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#5558" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="5560" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#5560" class="Bound">A</a><a id="5561" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5563" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5564" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#5564" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="5566" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5568" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#5558" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="5570" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#1025" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="5572" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#5560" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="5574" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#1203" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="5576" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#5560" class="Bound">A</a><a id="5577" class="Symbol">}</a>
      <a id="5585" class="Comment">------------------</a>
    <a id="5608" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5610" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#1635" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">μ</a> <a id="5612" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#5564" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="5614" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#4652" class="Datatype Operator">⟶</a> <a id="5616" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#5564" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="5618" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#3956" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="5620" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#1635" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">μ</a> <a id="5622" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#5564" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="5624" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#3956" class="Function Operator">]</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Two possible formulations of `μ`

    μ N  ⟶  N [ μ N ]

    (μ N) · V  ⟶  N [ μ N , V ]

    (μ (ƛ N)) · V  ⟶  N [ μ (ƛ N) , V ]

The first is odd in that we substitute for `f` a term that is not a value.

The second has two values of function type, both lambda abstractions and fixpoints.

    What if the body of μ must first reduce to a value? Two cases.

    Value is a lambda.

    (μ f → N) · V
      ⟶  (μ f → ƛ x → N′) · V
      ⟶  (ƛ x → N′) [ f := μ f → ƛ x → N ] · V
      ⟶  (ƛ x → N′ [ f := μ f → ƛ x → N ]) · V
      ⟶  N′ [ f := μ f → ƛ x → N , x := V ]

    Value is itself a mu.

    (μ f → μ g → N) · V
      ⟶ (μ f → μ g → N′) · V
      ⟶ (μ f → μ g → λ x → N″) · V
      ⟶ (μ g → λ x → N″) [ f := μ f → μ g → λ x → N″ ] · V
      ⟶ (μ g → λ x → N″ [ f := μ f → μ g → λ x → N″ ]) · V
      ⟶ (λ x → N″ [ f := μ f → μ g → λ x → N″ ])
            [ g := μ g → λ x → N″ [ f := μ f → μ g → λ x → N″ ] · V
      ⟶ (λ x → N″ [ f := μ f → μ g → λ x → N″ ]
            [ g := μ g → λ x → N″ [ f := μ f → μ g → λ x → N″ ]) · V
      ⟶ N″ [ f := μ f → μ g → λ x → N″ ]
             [ g := μ g → λ x → N″ [ f := μ f → μ g → λ x → N″ ]
             [ x := V ]

    This is something you would *never* want to do, because f and g are
    bound to the same function. Better to avoid it by building functions
    into the syntax, I expect.

## Reflexive and transitive closure

  <a id="_⟶*_._∎"></a><a id="7146" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#7146" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">_∎</a> <a id="7149" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7151" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="7153" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7154" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#7154" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7156" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#7156" class="Bound">A</a><a id="7157" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7159" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7160" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#7160" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="7162" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7164" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#7154" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="7166" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#1203" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="7168" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#7156" class="Bound">A</a><a id="7169" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="7177" class="Comment">--------</a>
    <a id="7190" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7192" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#7160" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="7194" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#7096" class="Datatype Operator">⟶*</a> <a id="7197" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plta/DeBruijn.md %}{% raw %}#7160" class="Bound">M</a>

## Values do not reduce

Values do not reduce.

As a corollary, terms that reduce are not values.
